ARIE vol.045, 1922-1923


A.--List of copper-plates examined during the year 1922-23.
1
Placement
Government Epigraphist forIndia.
Year
…
King
…
Date
Mēsha of theyear withJupiter inṚishabha.
Language and Script
Tamil in Vaṭṭeḻuttu
Remarks
Damaged and sense obscure. Seems to recorda gift of land and money by one Vaḍa Nāyarof Pūdavāḍi for worship and offerings in thetemple of Tirunelli-Āḷvāṉ. The land andmoney were left in charge of different indivi-duals for the supply of the necessary rice,oil, fruits, etc.
2
Placement
Do.
Year
…
King
…
Date
Makara of theyear withJupiter inKaṟkaṭaka.
Language and Script
Tamil in Vaṭṭeḻuttu
Remarks
Records a gift of 35 kaḻañju of gold for burn-ing a perpetual lamp in the temple of Dēva-dēvēśaṉ Tiruvaḍi at Tirunelli by a certainKōdai Ïrāmanāya... of Vaḷḷuva-nāḍu.The dēvakarmis of Nelkkuṉṟam, includingthe Paṇḍāravāriyar, received the gold andundertook to provide for the burning of thelamp by commuting its interest in paddyinto that of oil from the residents of Iḷam-bilāchchēri.

5
Placement
Mr. Rm.St.Sivanandam Pillai,Kumbhakonām, throughMr.P.V.Jagadisa Ayyar.
Year
Pallava
King
Kō-Vijaya-Nandivikrama-varman.
Date
61st year
Language and Script
Grantha & Tamil
Remarks
Gift of 16 vēli of land free of taxes in Nalgūrnewly constituted into a brahmadēya villagecalled Paṭṭattāḷmaṅgalam to a number ofBrāhmaṇas at the request of Maṅgala-nāḍāḷvāṉ. This included the 12 vēli of landalready granted as brahmadēya in the 59thyear of the king. The ājñapti was Vijaya-nallūḻāṉ of Ālappākkam. The engraver ofthese plates was Śrī Daṇḍi, son of Viḍēlvi-ḍugu Pallavapperundachchaṉ of Aimbaṉiach-chēri of Kachchippēḍu.
6
Placement
Mr. M.N.Srinivasacharya,the late Panditi of this office.
Year
Vijayanagara
King
Veṅkaṭapatirāya-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1513,Khara, Āshā-ḍha, śu.,paurṇimā,Lunar ec-lipse.
Language and Script
Sanskrit (Nandināgarī)
Remarks
Records the gift by the king, of the villageKāyāru with its hamlet (upagrāma) calledVaḍakkuppaṭṭu, situated in Raṇḍāyiram-vēlipaṭṭu in Kumuḷi-nāḍu a sub-division ofĀmūru-kōṭṭam in Paḍavīḍu-mahārājya andin Chaṅgaḷanīrpaṭṭu-sīmā, as sarvamānya tolearned Brāhmaṇas, divided into 84 sharesand surnamed Chañchasamudra. The grantwas made at the request (vijñapti) of thegeṇeral (sēnēśa) Cheṁchabhūpa who wasthe son of the chief (bhūpāla) Ahōbalēśa andthe Governor of Chandragiri and other forts.Among the donees were many scholarslearned in grammar (śabda-śāstra) andastronomy (jyōtisha).
7
Placement
Do.
Year
Do.
King
Veṅkaṭapatirāya
Date
Saka 1534,Parīdhāvi,Māgha, śu.saptamī.
Language and Script
Sanskrit, (Nandinagari)
Remarks
Records the gift of the village Muruga-maṅgalam surnamed Gōpālaśrīsamudrasituated in the Paḍavīḍu-mahārājya,Toṇḍīra-maṇḍala, Cheṅgalippaṭṭu-sīmā,Raṇḍāyirapaṭṭu, Kumuḷi-nāḍu and Āmūri-kōṭṭa as sarvamānya to the scholar, Rāma-kṛishṇa-jōsya of the Harita-gōtra, Āpas-tamba-sūtra, and Yajuś-śākhā who was wellversed in the Vēdas, Vēdāṅgas, Tarka (logic),Smṛiti and Sūryasiddhanta, and who was theson of Mallikārjunārādhya and Gaṅgāmbikāand the grandson of Liṅganārādhya of theSvaramaṇḍala family. The grant was madein the presence of the god Veṅkaṭēśa.

Placement
Mr. Uruma SivasankaraRao through Mr. A.Ranga-swamy Sarasvati of thisoffice.
Year
…
King
…
Date
…
Language and Script
Sanskrit, (Nāgarī)
Remarks
Records the grant by Triṇayana-Pallava ofthe village Lavaṇapura (Uppuṭūru) toseveral Erāhmaṇas of the Yājñavalkya seetwhose names and respective shares areenumerated. This grant seems to have beenengraved during the time of the Vijaya-nagara king Vijaya-Bhūpati.
9
Placement
The late Mr. K.V.Laksh-mana Rao, M.A., TeluguEncyclopaedia Office,Egmere.
Year
Reḍḍi
King
Anna-Vēma (entitled) Vīra-Nārāyaṇa.
Date
Śaka 1293,Rādhā (i.e.,Vaiśākha),Lunar eclipse.
Language and Script
Sanskrit (in Telugu) & Telugu
Remarks
States that the king succeeded his brother An-na-Pōta to his ancestral throne. Records there-grant to several brahmans of the villageUppugallu which had been resumed sometime previously. The names and gōtras ofthe donees with their respective shares areenumerated. The inscription was composedby Bālasarasvatī.

14
Placement
The late Mr. K.V.LakshmanaRao, M.A., Secretary, TeluguAcademy, Madras.

WesternChāḷukya.

Date

Sanskrit in Archaic Telugu

15
Placement
The Collector of Kistna
Year
Reḍḍi
King
Anna-Vēma
Date
Śaka 1293,Pausha, ba. 5,Saturday,Makara-(Saṁkra-mana).
Language and Script
Sanskrit & Telugu in Telugu
Remarks
Records the gift of the village Drujjavaramsurnamed as Annavēmapura on the banks ofthe river Malāpahā in the Kurttidēśa by theking, to the brahman Appayārya who wasthe purōhita of the king and to his threeyounger brothers Śrīrāma-Bhaṭṭa, Pinnaya-Bhaṭṭa, and Sūri-Bhaṭṭa. These were thesons of Allāḍa-Bhaṭṭa and belonged to theŚrīvatsa-gōtra. Pinnaya-Bhaṭṭa is said tohave been the king's adviser on Dharma(i.e., law).

672
Placement
On a slab set up in the compoundof the Śambhuliṅgasvāmintemple at Siruguppa, Siru-guppa taluk, Bellary district.

WesternChāḷukya.

Tribhuvanamalladēva, ‘ruling at Kalyāṇa-pura.’
Date
Chāḷukya-Vikramayear 16, Prajā-pati, Kārtika,amāvāsye, Sun-day.
Language and Script
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records gifts of lands made at the villages Siruguppe,Siriyūru and Koḷanūru to the god Svayambhu-Kētalēś-varadēva of Siruguppe, by Abhinavasarasvatī Piriya-Kētaladēvī, the quesn of Tribhuvanamalladēva, for theofferings of the god and for the maintenance of the templeservants. It also states that Mahāsāmanta ManneyaChokarasa of the Sinda family who was the lord ofBhōgāvatīpura, made provision for feeding brahmans.The queen is stated to have been governing the said threevillages, which were situated in the subdivision Tekke-kallu Twelve.

779
Placement
On the Nandi-pillar planted beforethe Amarēśvara temple in thesame village.
Year
…
King
…
Date
Kali 2000 (?) Ardhō-daya.
Language and Script
Sanskrit (prose & verse) in Telugu & Telugu
Remarks
Purports to record the grant of the village Lavanapura(Uppuṭūru) to 1,000 brahmans who were the followers ofYājñavalkya and who are said to have come from thetown Ahichchhatrapura on the banks of the Ganges, byTrinētra-Pallava. Also records the measurements of thestreets called Sōmavīdhi and Sūryavīdhi as well as thehouse-sites that were presented and the garden and thearable lands allotted to each share. It also records certainagreements made between the shareholders as to sellingshares in the village to outsiders and receiving dowries forgirls in marriage. Separate shares were allotted to thegods Mahādēva, Kēśava and Vighnēśvara and to the god-dess Pādāmbikāśaktī. The extent of the village and itsboundaries are given at great length and with minutedetails. See C.P.No. 8 of Appendix A above.

Śaka, 1131, Mēsha-Saṁkrānti.
Language and Script
Sanskrit in Telugu & Telugu
Remarks
Records the confirmation made by the king of an earliergrant of the village Iḍupulapāḍu in Karma-rāshṭra madeby Triṇayana-Pallava to Brāhmaṇas of various gōtraswho were learned in the Vēdas and were the followers ofthe Kātyāyana-sūtra and the Kāṇva-śākhā. The namesof the donees and their respective shares are enumerated.
